Citywide Health Education Exhibition

▲Scheduled to Be Held at Puyi Society from June 1st to 3rd

▲Various Health Performances and Lectures Will Be Held at the Same Time

The citywide health education exhibition organized by the Shanghai Municipal Education and Health Bureaus has been decided to be held at Puyi Society on Zixia Street, Dadongmen, from June 1st to 3rd. The organization of the association is divided into two major departments: general affairs and exhibits. The exhibit part is divided into three groups: schools, society, and reference, with Zhou Feicheng, Chen Bai, and Wu Liguo serving as directors. The general affairs department is also divided into three groups, including affairs, storage, and publicity. The directors of each group are Sun Jiaqi, Zhou Shang, and Hu Changcai. The general affairs department held a meeting the other day, chaired by Zhou Shang and recorded by Shen Yijun. The main points are as follows: (1) Exhibits are divided into two categories: free participation and donation or recognition as a unit. (2) The exhibition opening hours are from 9:00 am to 5:00 pm every day. (3) All participants in the exhibition should go to the Education Bureau to collect or request by mail the exhibit catalog form on May 17th, fill in all the exhibits in detail, and send personnel to the Education Bureau to register with the exhibit catalog from May 21st to 27th, and receive labels for pasting. After counting, send the exhibits to the meeting two days before the opening (May 30th) from 2:00 pm. (4) During the exhibition, health lectures will be held, and the target audience will be divided into three types: (A) the public, (B) teachers, and (C) children. They will be held in the auditorium. (5) Children's performances will be held at the same time, and the scope includes: (A) hygienic habit activities, (B) first aid performances, (C) health story performances, (D) sports team performances of about 20 people, and (E) other health activity performances. (6) Another room will be opened to show health education films. (7) The affairs of the children's creative health picture exhibition will be handled by the painting solicitation group. (8) Entrance tickets are divided into movie tickets and children's performance tickets. No entrance tickets are required for the general assembly and lectures.

National Games Organizing Committee Passes National Martial Arts Competition Rules

(Tokyo, 11th) The Organizing Committee of the National Games held a standing committee meeting on the evening of the 10th, chaired by Chu Minyi. Resolutions: 1. Approved the national martial arts competition rules, along with other rules, to be distributed to various units for use as soon as possible. 2. 5. Regardless of whether the manuscript is published or not, it will not be returned. However, if advance notice is given and sufficient return postage is included, it can be done accordingly. Please also include return postage for inquiries.

Researching wireless radio emphasizes experimentation, and materials are essential for experimentation. In major commercial ports, purchasing materials is not difficult, but in remote outer areas, mechanical materials are often not easy to obtain. To facilitate those interested in research, this publication has conducted a detailed survey of the products of various companies. Those who wish to purchase wireless radios or need materials should send a detailed list of their requirements to the Wireless Radio Weekly Department of Shen Bao, and we will contact the relevant parties on their behalf and provide detailed price information for direct purchase from the companies. When purchasing, mentioning that you were introduced by this publication may result in favorable pricing. It is also possible to entrust this publication to make the purchase on your behalf. This publication acts entirely in the service of readers and does not charge any handling fees. Please take note.

Multiple Radios Use One Antenna

— Zhong Qin

In the wireless radio field, although antennas are extremely disliked, and various methods are sought to avoid installing them, it is universally acknowledged that antennas should not be avoided simply because they are troublesome. So far, no inventor in the wireless radio field has discovered an absolutely foolproof method to eliminate antennas. If more than one radio is installed in public places or hotels, wouldn't it require installing many antennas? The wireless radio community has been discussing how to avoid this difficulty for a long time without finding a perfect solution.

Recently, this long-debated problem has gradually reached a conclusion: the first way to avoid installing multiple antennas is to have several radios share one antenna. In other words, one antenna is responsible for receiving radio waves for multiple radios. This is the only method, and it is gradually being improved and will eventually be realized.

Having one antenna responsible for receiving radio waves from the air for multiple radios is not very precise. This was the conclusion drawn from initial experiments. Because multiple radios each receive radio waves of different wavelengths, the branching is very complex. In the initial test, using two radios with one antenna did not yield good results and was difficult to adjust. Lengthening the antenna did not improve the performance. Later, a capacitor with a capacitance of approximately 0.0002 was added between the antenna and the ground, and the results improved significantly. After testing with two radios, then three, then four, a general conclusion was reached: the number of radios sharing one antenna for receiving radio waves must be limited. However, the standard for determining this limit has not yet been determined. Initially, the only limit was five radios sharing a 20-foot-long antenna. If six radios were used, no sound could be received. Also, the wavelength limit is related to the number of radios. In the initial experiments, five six-tube radios sharing one antenna could only receive radio waves within a range of 200 to 600 meters. The reason for this is still unclear.

Later, through gradual improvement and research, a British radio expert increased the number of radios to fifty, all sharing one antenna, and the results were excellent. Because removing the antenna halved the sound volume, while installing it doubled the volume and increased the range, it proved that he had truly succeeded. His method also involved adding a capacitor between the antenna and the ground, but the antenna was relatively high. Philips has now hired this radio expert as an engineer, and he is still making improvements. Perhaps there will be even more surprising developments in the future!

Wiring of Center-Tapped Resistors

— Qing

Center-tapped resistors should be directly connected to the filaments (as shown in Figure A). If they are connected to the output of the power transformer (as shown in Figure B), even if the two wires AB are slightly different in length, the voltage at both ends will be unbalanced, which can easily cause AC hum. Similarly, using the center tap of the power transformer without using a center-tapped resistor can also cause the same problem. Also, the filament regulator of an AC radio should be connected before the center-tapped resistor (as shown in Figure C). Notice for Radio Operators (1) ()

— Ti Gan

Procedures for Radio Communication

(1) All communication times specified by the Radio Administration Bureau must be strictly observed and not delayed.

(2) When it is time for Station A and Station B to communicate, they should call each other promptly. In the case of simplex stations, one side must call while the other listens. If Station B hears the signal from Station A, it must wait until Station A has finished calling before replying and requesting that Station A begin transmitting. In the case of duplex stations, which can transmit and receive simultaneously, both sides should listen while calling to avoid delays.

(3) If Station A calls Station B, and there is no response from the other side for a long time, causing a delay in the communication time, it should be recorded in the logbook and reported to the chief radio operator to investigate the cause.

(4) In cases where both sides have difficulty receiving the signal, the wavelength should be changed, and the other party should be notified immediately using a simple phrase to avoid misunderstandings.

(5) If neither Station A nor Station B has any telegrams to transmit during the communication period, they should still monitor each other. If Station A has a significant backlog of telegrams with Station C, Station A can notify Station B to wait temporarily while it communicates with Station C for a certain period.

(6) After the telegram transmission has begun, if the communication time is about to end, the decision to stop or continue transmitting and receiving should be based on the urgency and length of the telegrams.

(7) If Station A still has several urgent telegrams to transmit when the communication between Station A and Station B is about to end, Station A must immediately request that Station B continue monitoring. Station B should continue monitoring for another ten minutes. If further extension is needed, Station B should inquire with Station C, whose communication time is within the scheduled period, to see if an accommodation can be made before making a final decision.

(8) If there are any aspects of the communication time that do not conform to the needs of radio operations, the chief radio operator should report the situation to the Radio Administration Bureau for modification.

A Cost-Free Morse Code Practice Device

— Li Yuanqing

Radio enthusiasts hate AC hum the most, but here we are using AC hum to create a Morse code practice device.

As shown in the diagram, a cord is wound around the cord of an electric lamp (about twenty or thirty turns). The other end is connected in series with a headset and a telegraph key, and then grounded. When the telegraph key is opened and closed, a pleasant telegraph signal can be heard in the headset.

Small Experiences

— Xu Bing

White lines on dials and bakelite panels that have become soiled over time can be cleaned by mixing a small amount of white lead powder with linseed oil to form a thick paste, and then applying it to the lines. After it dries, it will be as clean and white as new.

Using sandpaper to remove the insulation from copper wire is cleaner and less likely to cut the wire than using a knife.

If you want to know the thickness of the copper wire you are using but do not have a wire gauge, you can use the following method to measure it: wind the copper wire you want to measure tightly around a pencil for one inch. After knowing the number of turns per inch, you can look up its gauge and size in a copper wire table (wire tables are found in electrical engineering and radio reference books). For example, if an enameled wire has 17 turns per inch, you can find in the table that it is a No. 15 wire with a diameter of .0589 inches.

Radio Troubleshooting and Solutions (4)

— AA

(4) Noise Generation

There are two types of noise: noise generated within the radio itself and noise from external interference. If noise persists even after disconnecting the antenna and ground, it is a problem with the radio itself. Otherwise, it is external interference.

Here, we will focus on examining noise generated within the radio itself.

Noise is a most unwelcome sound that can disrupt excellent programming and spoil enjoyment. If your radio is generating noise, you can try checking it according to the table above.

Next time, we will discuss sound fidelity.

Spring and Autumn

Firefighting

— Baihe

Casually tossing a cigarette butt, which happened to land in a pile of cotton wool, a spark can start a prairie fire, immediately causing smoke to rise through the roof and flames to soar into the sky. Therefore, the moment I hear a hubbub of voices and chaotic siren wails, I'm frightened to the point where my teeth start chattering, afraid that a fire in a neighbor's house will spread to my own, forcing me to rush out with disheveled hair and hastily donned cap to help put it out. If the fire is still a good distance away from my house, then I don't need to worry, I just squeeze into the crowd and crane my neck to watch. It's not that I like to make a fool of myself, it's just that under heaven, everyone is like this.

Our Shenyang caught a spark, and in one night, it burned down the two provinces of Liaoning and Jilin. The fire was so intense that Heilongjiang in the north and Jinzhou in the south immediately turned into piles of rubble. Then, it burned to Shanhaiguan and the entire territory of Rehe. The fire was extraordinarily fierce, and the neighbors standing by with folded arms were all amazed, praising it as a sight to behold. Later, the fire in northern Manchuria gradually threatened to destroy the Chinese Eastern Railway and spread into Russian territory, so Russia prepared firefighting equipment to block its path. The fire in Shanhaiguan gradually approached the Kailuan Mines along the Beining Railway, so Britain immediately cut off its path. The raging fire, blocked on this route, followed the wind and spread to the corner of Chahar.

When Shenyang first caught fire, China sounded the alarm and sought help from the Geneva fire department. Unexpectedly, the firefighters pushed responsibility onto each other, and no one was willing to take action. Later, they reluctantly took action, but unfortunately, the fire had already spread out of control, and pouring water on it was like pouring oil, making it impossible to extinguish. But this fire was indeed too severe, scorching even those watching it across the Pacific, who couldn't stand it anymore. So the Washington fire department prepared to help the Geneva fire department put out the fire together. Although it's uncertain whether they can put out the fire in one go, I think a fire department, even if it's not very effective, is still better than using buckets to draw water for firefighting. At least it can suppress the fire and gradually extinguish it.

Everyone, watch the fire department put out the fire with folded arms.

Beauty

— Cai Lian

Calling a woman beautiful is said to be "red beauty," this phrase is seen in the Emperor Wu of Han's essay: "Wrapped in red beauty yet not made clear," passed down to this day, still with its meaning.

There are very few women who can be called "red beauty", even those recorded in history are few in number. However, who does not want their appearance to surpass others? Who does not want to enjoy the beautiful name of "red beauty"? Precisely because it is so precious, everyone's desire to be a "red beauty" becomes more urgent.

Today's general modern ladies and modern grandmothers have misunderstood the meaning of the two words "red beauty." They think that the meaning of the word "face" is, in the Book of Songs: "Face like a shiny lacquer", interpreted as forehead; in the Book of Rites: "Correct color" interpreted as between the eyebrows, literally, "red beauty" means a red face, thinking that people with red faces can be regarded as red beauties. When girls are shy or frightened, two red clouds occasionally float on their cheeks. Su Shi's poem "Red tide climbs the cheeks, drunk betel nut" this kind of natural grace can indeed make poets sing without end. Unfortunately, it is very temporary, and after shyness or fear, the two red clouds also dissipate. Therefore, in order to keep the red face staying on their faces for a long time, modern women must use artificial methods. What is the artificial method? It is to apply red to the cheeks.

They do not count how old they are? How good is their appearance? Even if their faces are as ugly as yakshas, ​​and as old as Xu Niang, they also learn from others, tightly holding a mirror, applying expensive Parisian powder, and then desperately applying a layer of scarlet rouge, impolitely claiming to be "red beauty."

Since modern women advocate this in cities, naturally village girls will imitate them in the countryside. In this way, in a few years, all women will definitely be "red beauties." Oh, what a grand sight!

As the saying goes: "Red beauty has been ill-fated since ancient times." Since modern women are so presumptuous in claiming to be "red beauty", aren't they afraid of the worries of ill-fatedness?

Public Cemetery

— Yun Sun

The black monster that devours life certainly inspires some fear, but even the rows of desolate graves, a mound of yellow earth, cannot but stir up agitation and fear. In the past, the cemeteries privately operated by feudal lords and prime ministers were naturally opulent and magnificent. However, no consideration was given to economic land use. Archways of honor and the erection of stone figures of men and horses often cost millions. Currently, wealthy people also have pre-burial constructions, but these are beyond the imagination of middle-class families. Recently, I participated in the funeral ceremony of a deceased friend and had the opportunity to tour a public cemetery. Because I was one of the members in charge of the funeral arrangements, I went in the morning to prepare a simple hall, carefully examined and observed everything.

Upon entering, there was a funeral home, and next to the funeral home was a small hall. Every few feet, the tomb areas were connected by paved cement walkways that were so clean and flat they were almost reflective. There were green grasses and lush lawns, as well as red flowers and green trees. When we imagine its scenery in the seasons of spring flowers and autumn moons, it makes people want to linger and forget to return. Each tombstone and each pagoda were crafted with ingenuity, with different degrees of exquisiteness. The ornate pagoda tops were even topped with a small angel or a Maitreya-like human god. Analyzing many of the remaining portraits, there were stern fathers, kind mothers, beloved sons, beautiful daughters, youthful beauties, and handsome young men. That day, I saw a woman in her forties bringing her daughter-in-law to sweep the grave of her deceased husband. Holding a bouquet of fresh flowers, she instructed her daughter-in-law to offer them to her husband, and then asked her son to take photos of the tomb pagoda. The three stood side by side and paid their respects, then slowly walked out of the public cemetery, saying, "The empty space on the right is where I will rest in peace. Remember it." The thing that swallowed my friend's life was a yellow monster in disguise. It was brought down from the hearse and carried into the tomb gate by several Boy Scouts. The ceremony was very simple. The pastor prayed, everyone sang two hymns, and then the ceremony was declared complete. We know that baptized Christians always express a clean and silent demeanor everywhere, so a large public cemetery like this, every blade of grass and every leaf, seems to be spotless. Outside the gate, there is the poetic beauty of clear streams and winding paths, and the familiar sounds of chickens and dogs. On the iron fence hangs a small sign that says "Baptist Public Cemetery," which also seems to carry a somber component. This kind of place can only be described as the grave path of the human world and the paradise of the ghost world.

Humorous Remarks

— Zui Chi Sheng (Drunk Fool)

Emptying the country with aviation! The government and the people have been shouting the slogan "Saving the country with aviation" for a long time. "Naming the son before he's born," Airplane numbers □□. If those numbers were compiled, it would be quite a sight. However, according to reports on the success of fundraising for aviation funds, it is still far from the planned amount. In particular, wealthy people have donated very little, which is bound to be disappointing. As for the front lines, the enemy planes are committing atrocities, and the suffering of the military and civilians is truly indescribable. Our country's existing air force must be used to suppress bandits and cannot participate in combat. (According to reports, the air force's bombing of Zhu De and Mao Zedong has been quite effective.) And the future air force is not yet known when it can be established. This kind of "saving the country with aviation" is afraid that it will turn into "emptying the country with aviation"!

Be mindful of the national crisis! Now is the moment when the "national crisis is upon us"! But the people in the cities are still playing and enjoying themselves as usual. The entertainment venues everywhere are still full to the brim. It's as if the national crisis, no matter how urgent, has nothing to do with me. The ethnicity of the Yellow Emperor Hua Wei is so bad, I really want to imitate Jia Yi's wailing. However, according to what I think, the mentality of ordinary people is because the national crisis is upon us, clearly it is; the national crisis is still at the beginning. The time is not ripe, and it has not reached the focal point. In case it comes to "be mindful of the national crisis," or "the national crisis is at your feet," then that will be the urgent moment!

Long Novel

Fourth Company Commander of Northeast China

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter Six: Sweet and Bitter Love Affairs Coolly Observed from Two Sides, Rugged Worldly Path Secretly Promised for Three Years

Ji Zhi nodded repeatedly in agreement. Gui Zhi said, "Why don't you have a holiday during the New Year?" Ji Zhi said, "We celebrate the Gregorian calendar New Year, don't you know?" Gui Zhi said, "But then again, there's nothing to do in Haidian, it's better to be in the office doing official business, which can kill time." Ji Zhi smiled and said, "It's always good to rest. It's so windy, running around, it's cold and uncomfortable." These words were all

said to be boring, the two faced each other, not knowing what to do. Gui Zhi did not say he was leaving, and Ji Zhi didn't want to leave him and go home alone. So he smiled and said to him, "The coffee shop is not closed, shall we go have another cup of coffee?" This hit Gui Zhi's fancy, which shows that the words of a confidant are always guessed right, and he smiled and said, "I don't know how to drink coffee, why do you always invite me to drink coffee." Ji Zhi said, "If you don't want to drink coffee, then wait a day..." Gui Zhi, before he finished speaking, said, "It's the New Year, you're inviting me, and I can't refute your words, so I'll accompany you to sit down." As he spoke, he moved his feet and walked first. Ji Zhi looked at him and couldn't tell what he meant, so he had to let him go all the way to the cafe. In this cafe, there were originally only two booths, one inside was already occupied, and the two sat in the booth outside. Ji Zhi sat down and smiled, "I think it's still the old rules, should I order a bowl of lotus root flour for you?" As he said this, he heard someone in the booth next door say, "Huh?" Listening carefully, the sound on that side was silent again. Of course, there was nothing surprising about saying to order a bowl of lotus root flour. Perhaps that "huh" from the people next door wasn't directed at him, so there was no need to pay attention to it. The waiter brought the coffee and lotus root flour, and the two sat facing each other across the table, slowly eating and drinking. Gui Zhi didn't speak, so Ji Zhi didn't say anything either. The room was silent for a while, and Ji Zhi was the first to open his mouth and said, "How was your New Year?" Gui Zhi said, "What's good? On New Year's Eve, I was almost forced to death by the creditors." He said he was poor, and Ji Zhi couldn't comfort him, so he just said faintly, "It's the same in that world." After saying this, they were silent again (68)

Small Gardening

Summer Flowers

— Zhu Chuo

"Once the Rubus parvifolius flower blooms, the floral season is over." Indeed, as the roses release their delicate and vibrant petals, all the flowers and trees on the earth have already faded in their green and red hues. Plums, those button-like fruits, are already densely packed on the branches; cherries have reddened, and water caltrop has greened. The flowing light, like water, has already secretly sent away the brilliant spring, replacing it with the youthful beauty of summer. During this transition from spring to summer, there are many flowers that are worth cherishing, like a maiden in her seventeen years of beauty.

The elegant and faint fragrance of orchids gently wafts into the senses, certainly not comparable to the strong and greasy fragrances of perfumes like "4711" or "Tosca"! The orchid truly deserves the title of "national fragrance." As spring fades, families in the Jiangnan region reverently display orchids; before one even steps into the room, the sweet fragrance already envelops the senses. The orchids that bloom in spring include both Cymbidium goeringii and Cymbidium faberi. Cymbidium faberi are mostly sold in the market by people from Shaoxing. Cymbidium goeringii has thinner and fewer leaves, and the types of flowers are also more numerous. The plain heart, plum petal, lotus petal, and black heart varieties of Cymbidium goeringii are all very precious, and their value is naturally very high. Moreover, because orchids are flowers planted in pots, cultivation is not easy. The pot, soil, water, and moss all require meticulous study. A slight mistake can cause them to wither and die.

Peonies truly deserve the reputation of "national beauty." The bowl-sized blossoms are crimson, purplish, and every color imaginable. The color is so vibrant and magnificent that they truly dominate all other flowers. Peonies with black petals are the most precious, followed by green, and red is the most common. The Peide Hall Funeral Home outside the阊 Gate of Suzhou, with its "five-colored peonies," was once very famous, so many tourists carrying wine would come to admire them. But now, after many changes, it is unknown whether the peonies there still have their former glory. The flowering period of peonies is short, and they must be picked immediately after they are in full bloom, otherwise, they will not bloom again next year. Therefore, there is a Suzhou proverb: "Pick peonies three days after Grain Rain," which probably matches the saying "Good flowers don't last long."

Wisteria's clusters of dazzling flowers, like缨絡, hang among the tender green branches, even more crystal clear and dazzling than purple grapes, worthy of lingering admiration. As spring comes to an end, wisteria is truly a lovely flower. In the courtyard of the Fengzhi Guild Hall (Humble Administrator's Garden) in Suzhou, there is an ancient wisteria planted by Wen Zhengming, a famous person of the Ming Dynasty. The vine trunk is gnarled, and the branches are scattered. When it is flowering, it is even more delicately expressing that it is a relic of the sages.

Hydrangeas are as white as snow and as round as balls; hydrangeas truly decorate the gardens of early summer with much magnificent scenery. Although the hydrangea blossoms are so large, if you look closely, they are actually many small flowers clustered together. This can truly be called a flower with a sense of collectivity.

Aglaia odorata and Chloranthus inconspicuus Although their colors are not enough to move people, their faint and fragrant aroma is sweet, pure, and lovely, enough to make people infatuated. These two types of flowers can not only be planted in pots to be displayed indoors, but also be dried and placed in tea leaves to add a light fragrance to the tea. When brewing tea and chatting leisurely, the rich aroma permeates from the cup. Slowly sipping it, one doesn't even need Lu Tong's seven bowls to feel a breeze under the armpits and be like an immortal!

Roses have excellent color, fragrance, and taste. The thorny rose truly lives up to its name. The delicate red color, the rich fragrance, and the petals can not only be soaked in wine, but also mashed and mixed with white sugar to make rose candy and rose jam. Rose candy is certainly sweet and delicious, but the delicate, bright red rose jam, smeared on white zongzi, even makes gourmets' appetites stir. It adds a layer of charm to the Dragon Boat Festival.

The flowers of early summer, in addition to the above-mentioned varieties, also include climbing roses, honeysuckle, roses, and other flowers, which, like flowing water, bloom in an instant, from tiny calyxes to a riot of color like brocade. But after a few storms, the path is already full of fallen petals, and the ground is covered with remnants of red. Flowers bloom and wither, but it's only for a moment. However, life follows this flowing light, from young to strong, from strong to old. Looking at these flowers that wither easily, one truly feels that "Time, time, will never come again," especially during this time of national crisis, how can we let it pass by idly!

Recent News on Silk, Tea, and Sericulture in Jiangsu and Zhejiang

(Changzhou) In various towns and villages, the number of farmers unable to raise silkworms this year is increasing. Mulberry trees are budding later due to the cold weather, causing a delay in the silkworm season. Silkworm farmers, lacking the funds to purchase silkworm eggs, are borrowing from township offices to buy and raise improved breeds. After hatching, the weather has been sunny and warm, and the silkworms are developing well. However, due to economic factors, there is a wide disparity in the progress of the silkworm season. The earliest silkworms in the southwest villages are already in the "large eye" stage, while in the eastern villages, the majority of silkworms are beginning to feed after their third molt, and in the northern villages, the latest silkworms have just begun their third molt.

(Yuhang) In areas such as Pingyao and Changle Bridge, farmers who incubated local breeds early in the season have almost completely discarded them. Although the improved breeds raised as replacements are starting later, the sunny and warm weather has been conducive to their development. Furthermore, instructors are assisting in the process, ensuring that the silkworms are progressing very well. However, the silkworm season is uneven, with some early silkworms already emerging from their cocoons and ready to spin their silk, while others are just beginning to feed after their fourth molt, and the latest hatchlings are still beginning to feed after their third molt.

### Silk Cocoon Merchants Request Tax Exemption and Relief

Telegraphic Request for Exemption of Various Taxes to Lighten the Burden

Recently, silk cocoon merchants in this city have reported a slump in the sales of raw silk by foreign firms, causing silk prices to plummet. The price of Grade B white filature silk has fallen to 500 taels. At this price, the cost of raw materials for each 100 catties of fresh cocoons is only worth just over 20 yuan. As the new cocoons from Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces are about to enter the market, if the government does not provide tax exemption and relief, the economies of both farmers and merchants are bound to go bankrupt. Therefore, the Silk Cocoon General Association and the Silk Factory Association have telegraphed the governments and finance departments of Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces, requesting exemption from cocoon trade business tax, stamp tax, inspection fees, education fees, and local public welfare donations in order to lighten the burden and maintain the livelihoods of farmers and merchants.

### High-Grade Green Tea Sales to France Continue Smoothly

A total of 629 boxes were purchased by firms such as Jardine Matheson, Concordia, Jinlong, and Tianyu. "Zhen Mei" tea sold for 100 to 150 yuan, while "Zhen Mei" needle tea sold for 43 to 62 yuan, with no change from the previous day. However, as various foreign firms are already packing and exporting new goods, it is expected that future purchases will be more conservative in pricing.

### Food: Rice Prices in He Xia Fall by 10-20 Cents

(South Shanghai) Yesterday, 50-60 sources arrived. However, due to wavering confidence, the market for both retail and wholesale rice remained sluggish. Although the situation improved slightly, the market was still stagnant due to the abundant supply. Consequently, the prices of "Su Tong" glutinous rice and "Nan Gang" rice continued to fall by 10-20 cents. Merchants mostly purchased over a thousand bags of thin rice from Nanyang and Xinghua, as well as "Qing Jiao", "Songjiang", "Fengxi", and "Lian", but remained demanding, refusing to accept unless the price was lowered. As a result, the market price for thin rice fell by ten cents, while medium-quality rice fell by approximately twenty cents. This sluggish market was unexpected, and there is no expectation of a turnaround. "Du Yang Jian" rice continued to soften by several points, while "Yin Yuan" also fell by ten cents. "Bian Yuan" rice was able to hold steady due to a lack of supply.

(North Shanghai) Yesterday, about 30 sources arrived from the He Xia region. The market for white glutinous rice was weak, and prices fell by 10-20 cents. Thin rice of high quality fell by nearly 10 cents. The supply of early rice was strong, but demand was sluggish, and prices also fell by 10-20 cents. The supply of "Yang Jian" rice continued, and sales were good at the opening price. Medium and lower qualities were down by 10 cents. "Du Jian" rice was down by 10 cents, while "Ke Jian" rice was weak. "Yin Bian Yuan" rice showed signs of weakness.

▲ Correction: Yesterday's report stated that the market bushel was enlarged by 6.81 deciliters. Today, a letter from the Bean and Rice Trade Association states that the Association uses the standard bushel calibrated by the Inspection Bureau and that the Bureau sends personnel to supervise, making it impossible to enlarge or shrink the bushel in any way. This correction is made with utmost urgency.

### Oil Market: Hongtong Oil Lacks Momentum

Hongjiang tung oil is currently in its sales season. However, in recent years, due to the bankruptcy of the rural economy, domestic sales have declined year after year, and the annual production cannot be sold out. The fundamental problem for the past 3-4 years has been the oversupply. Hongtong oil is made from white tung oil and is exclusively used for painting and varnishing in China. It has no other uses and no foreign markets, limiting its sales and application. Based on current sales, unless production decreases, there will be an annual surplus, and there is fundamentally no solution. Even with the current sales season in summer, the market is as quiet as if it were off-season. Even if prices are loosened, they cannot attract buyers. This is due to the economic limitations of farmers, who cannot afford to engage in decoration. Secondary brands such as Yang Hengyuan and Qingyuanfeng are only selling for slightly over 21 yuan per barrel, and the market situation still has no potential for development.

Free Talk

### The World Gone Mad

— Jingzi

Reading the petition submitted by lawyer ×× on behalf of prisoners to the Ministry of Justice to investigate the long-standing malpractices of ××× Prison in yesterday's newspaper filled me with nameless sorrow. It also reminded me of a friend who starved to death in prison two years ago—a young man swallowed up by darkness. It was also in ××× Prison, that dark world, that terrifying den of demons. As far as I know, my friend was a diligent student, a promising young man, who was arrested by the police and handed over to a certain military organization simply for initiating and organizing an academic research society, and was sentenced to more than three years in prison. He was already seriously ill when he was sent to ××× Prison; however, the "benevolent" doctor in the prison determined that his illness was feigned. His fellow prisoners requested the prison authorities to temporarily remove the shackles from his hands and feet, but it was never allowed. He struggled in agony under the scourge of disease and shackles, and spent the whole day breathing out low and miserable groans. Sometimes even his groans were suppressed by angry scolding and whipping, and he could only quietly wait for death, unable to make a sound. When he was obviously beyond saving, he was moved to another dark room to await "divine grace." Only then was he allowed to temporarily remove the shackles from his rotting hands and feet. But with the removal of the shackles, this young man, this prisoner, finally opened his eyes, let out a miserable laugh, and was utterly released—he sacrificed himself in the dark den of demons.

The tragic death of this friend is not worth mentioning, as there are countless young victims sacrificed under the shroud of darkness and terror. And this phenomenon is not unique to China; Japan, Germany, Italy, and the entire world are all like this. The recent beating to death of a certain Japanese writer by the police is an example right before our eyes.

The whole world has gone mad, and history has returned to the Middle Ages.

War, massacre, terror, imprisonment, destruction, the dance of demons, the groans of slaves, the whole world has gone mad—

"Killing" has replaced "freedom," and "arrest" and "imprisonment" have confined "will." This is the golden age of interventionism.

Electrocution, tiger benches, pepper water forced up the nose, forced confessions, beatings, and humiliations occur both inside and outside prisons. Some are seeking death but cannot find it, while others are grinning ferociously. This is what the world is like—civilization has gone bankrupt, barbarism has been resurrected, and a vast expanse of fog has enveloped the entire world.

This world, this century, the suffering of civilization, the catastrophe of mankind, the reversal of history—

What is ××× Prison? This world is also a dark and miserable large prison cage. Complain? Where can we go to complain?

### Doctor (Continued)

— Shizhen

He lay in that gloomy sickroom, enduring the early mornings and the late evenings, enduring the indifferent faces of those young disciples, hoping to escape from the clutches of the disease, but God had no pity on him, and the disease grew worse day by day. Finally, not only did the lung disease not diminish, but it also added new symptoms. His testicles were swollen. This alarmed the medical scholar, who came to see him in person. He said that this phenomenon was because the lung bacteria had been driven by the medicine to the testicles, so it was necessary to cut off one testicle, and once it was cut off, his lung disease could gradually improve. Thank God, if his words were true. At that time, I told this to another friend, who liked to tell jokes, and he said, "This doctor is probably not very skilled. According to him, the lung bacteria can be driven away, so why don't they drive the lung bacteria all the way to the soles of the feet and drop them on the ground, instead of driving them to that important place?"

At the same time, the medical scholar also introduced another famous surgical doctor. My old friend was carried from one hospital to another, and in less than thirty minutes, the surgery was performed. After resting for a week, he moved back to his old hospital. But his illness still did not improve, and soon, the only remaining testicle was still swollen. So the medical scholar had to come again in person. After his diagnosis, he said that the previous testicle had not been cut cleanly, and the remaining piece had congealed with the other good testicle, so the remaining one also had to be cut off. But the patient's body could not withstand it. The doctor naturally knew this better than we did. Cutting it off would probably lead to death sooner, while not cutting it off could prolong life for a few more days and allow for a peaceful death. So my friend and I both argued that we should not cut it off again.

Sure enough, after a few days, in the middle of one night, my friend breathed his last breath!—Let us bless this soul who struggled with illness for so long, may he rest in peace!

× × ×

My life has not been very long, and I have not seen many more abominable doctors' faces, but I have heard more cruel things. Do readers have the patience to hear me tell one or two more stories?

In Tokyo, a Japanese woman went to the Imperial University Hospital to see an eye doctor. Many assistants could not diagnose her disease. They invited the head of ophthalmology, who was also a very reputable old doctor. He opened the woman's eyelids up and down to look at them, and he understood, proud and satisfied. He was surrounded by a large group of intern students, who stood solemnly listening to their teacher's insights. The old doctor turned the woman's eyes and explained the cause of the disease to the students, pointing out the symptoms of the disease currently in the eyes, but he forgot the pain that the suffering woman was enduring under these circumstances.

The old doctor finished speaking triumphantly, giving the woman unparalleled glory, and personally dripped eye drops. But the woman's eyes had been tortured for so long and no longer obeyed her own control. Just as the eye drops were about to be dripped in, her eyes flashed with soreness and pain. The old doctor made several attempts but did not succeed. He lost his temper and slapped the woman's cheeks twice, threw the things down, and walked away in anger. The poor woman's eyes were dizzy, as if she had fainted. The students standing around looked in shock at the old doctor walking away and the woman with her eyes spinning, but no one dared to continue the surgery.

When the woman's consciousness became clear again, the young students told her to beg their teacher; in the end, the woman's smiling face and kneeling entreaties softened the old doctor's heart, and he came back to put in the drops again. "This is not unusual," the Japanese student who told me this story said, "because scientists are the noblest people in society!"

I have seen the authority of Japanese authoritative doctors, so I believe these words.

Slapping a woman heavily on the cheeks, although it is a great humiliation, is ultimately very different from taking a woman's life. Let me tell another story of an unfortunate woman who died at the hands of a cruel doctor.

The matter happened in Beiping, and many people knew about it at the time. I also do not want to announce the name of the hospital.

In a certain hospital in Beiping, a woman had a disease in her abdomen and had to undergo abdominal surgery. A famous doctor took on this job. This doctor's business had always been booming. One time, while he was performing surgery on this unfortunate woman, a call suddenly came from a certain important person summoning the doctor. The doctor thought only of the benefits he could get from seeing an important person once, so he forgot about the woman under his hands and casually told the assistants to sew up her belly. He got into a car and flew to the important person's house.

When the doctor returned, the woman had already died. The woman's family did not agree and demanded that the doctor reopen the abdomen to look. The abdomen was opened again, and in the intestines and stomach, a pair of scissors was found, which had been left inside because they had not been careful at the time!

This doctor had definite evidence of committing murder, but the laws of mankind did not punish him. I do not know why.

Therefore, I curse this doctor and all doctors who resemble him!

### Random Words from the Qu Cottage

— Zizhan

(26) What Year Is This?

What year is this? This is a foolish question that the intelligent people of our nation should be able to answer easily. If you ask a politician, the politician will surely say it is the year of constitutional government, where Zhuge Liang makes the laws and A Dou carries them out. If you ask a military strategist, the military strategist will surely say it is the year of suppressing bandits, where resistance against Japan need not be short-term, but can last for thousands upon thousands of years. Furthermore, if you ask an industrialist or merchant, they will say it is the year of domestic goods, as seen in the touching advertisements. If you ask an economist or agriculturist, they will say it is the year of rural revitalization, with special agencies already established. If you ask a thinker, they will say it is the year of widespread criticism, where Hu Shi has already become the target of arrows. If you ask an author, they will say it is the year of the author's autobiography, where self-narrated sorrows continue in clusters. If you ask a humorist, they will say it is the year of humor, where humorous articles spread like wildfire. As for me, I do not belong to any one school, but since I have taken up the pen to write, I will attach myself to the coattails of humor. What else can I say? What else is there to be humble about? However, humor comes from English, so it has the suspicion of being a foreign import. Since the national consciousness is astute, writing should avoid foreign allusions. We should remember our ancestors when citing precedents and love our country completely. Therefore, when I discuss humorous writers, I start with Confucius and Zhuang Zhou. Confucius and Zhuang Zhou lived during the Spring and Autumn and Warring States periods when the feudal lords were immoral and there were many taboos. One had to be humorous in order to open their mouths and write their pens. When the people of Zheng cursed Confucius as a homeless dog, Confucius accepted it happily. When people called Zhuang Zhou a cow or a horse, Zhuang Zhou would answer as a cow or a horse. The saints and sages like Confucius and Zhuang Zhou were not willing to be treated as dogs and horses, but they felt that in those chaotic times, people were worse than dogs and horses, so if they were called dogs and horses, they would simply be dogs and horses. Why should they argue? This is the humor of Confucius and Zhuang Zhou. However, Confucius aimed to pursue wealth and position, and he worked tirelessly to achieve this. Those who call themselves disciples of the sage often distort learning and pander to the world, aiding the wicked and abusing the tyrant, using their talent to steal a reputation and their intelligence to adorn evil. In every era, there have been people like Li Si and Feng Dao. Today's ambitious young people often

Curse the celebrities and scholars, saying, "This is so-and-so's running dog! This is so-and-so's party's running dog! This is so-and-so's class's running dog!" I don't know if these gentlemen have the magnanimity of Confucius and would say "Yes, yes," and happily accept it. This is why the humor of Confucius is unattainable and admirable. Now, there are writers who worship Confucius as the patron saint of humor, and there is good reason for this. Zhuang Zhou, on the other hand, willingly endured the humiliation of dragging his tail in the mud rather than taking office in the state, regarded the sage as a great thief, treated wealth and nobility as dirt, did not condemn right and wrong, and did not respect benevolence and righteousness. He saw the court of an immoral monarch and saw Jie in his heart; when he left the immoral wilderness, he met people who looked like Yi but had Zhi in their hearts. Why would he take the empty names of benevolence and righteousness and the undefined right and wrong? When he wrote, he felt that the world was mired in turbidity and could not be engaged with serious words. In today's language, it means that you cannot tell the truth in chaotic times. Therefore, he used "slanderous words" to expand, "heavy words" to convey truth, and "parables" to spread ideas. What are "slanderous words"? Long and verbose, boasting and exaggerating, flowery language, inexplicable mystery, like the speeches and declarations made by important figures. What are "heavy words"? In the past, writers quoted classics, "The Book of Songs says," "Confucius said." Today's commentators, if they do not quote Sun Yat-sen, Marx, then they quote Plekhanov, Lunacharsky, and so on. What are "parables"? Pointing at the mulberry tree and cursing the locust tree; hating the monk and beating the bald donkey: this is what today's poets and novelists excel at. Zhuang Zhou used these three elements to write, and Zhuang Zhou himself said that he used absurd theories, outrageous words, and unfounded expressions, sometimes indulging and not being bound, and not seeing himself as _. Humorous literature, this is the height of achievement. If the world were easily made orderly, Zhuang Zhou would probably not come out of this. Xun Qing said that in chaotic times, writing is hidden but colorful. These words are probably close to the truth. Alas, there are writers today who were born in this prosperous age but unfortunately are also known for their humor!

Red Carrot Whiskers

— Written by Jules Renard, Translated by Lin Qu

The Teakettle

Red Carrot Whiskers rarely had the chance to be useful to his family. He lurked in a corner, waiting for such an opportunity to arise. He listened without prejudice, and when the time came, he would emerge from the shadows, like a thoughtful person who alone remained calm among many troubled by passion, taking on the responsibility of directing everything.

He guessed that the Raypeak family needed clever and reliable help. Of course, she wouldn't tell him herself. She had too much self-respect. The agreement was formed in tacit understanding: Red Carrot Whiskers should act without encouragement and without expecting any reward, doing it all voluntarily.

He decided to get started.

From morning till night, a teakettle hung on the iron hook of the fireplace. In winter, when a lot of hot water was needed, the kettle was often filled and emptied, boiling over a large fire.

In summer, the water in the kettle was only needed after each meal to wash the dishes. The rest of the time, it boiled uselessly, constantly making soft chirping sounds, while two pieces of firewood smoldered beneath its cracked belly, almost extinguished.

Sometimes, Orolin no longer heard the chirping of the teakettle, so she would bend down and listen with her ear close.

"The water has all boiled away," she would say.

She would then take a bucket of water and pour it into the kettle, putting the two pieces of firewood together and stirring the ashes. After a while, the gentle song would rise again, and Orolin, relieved, would run off to do other things.

If someone said to her:

"Orolin, why are you boiling water you don't need? Take the kettle off and put out the fire. You're burning the firewood as if it didn't cost anything. When the weather gets cold, many poor people will be freezing to death without firewood, yet you are wasting resources. But you have always been a thrifty woman."

She would shake her head.

She had always seen a teakettle hanging on the fireplace hook.

She had always heard the sound of boiling water, whether it was raining, windy, or sunny. When the kettle was empty, she would fill it.

She now didn't even need to touch the kettle or look at it; she had memorized it in her heart. She only needed to listen. If the kettle made no sound, she would pour a bucket of water into it. She had become so accustomed to it, like stringing pearls, that she had never made a mistake.

Today, for the first time, she made a mistake.

The water poured onto the fire, and a cloud of ash, like a wild beast disturbed and enraged, pounced on Orolin, enveloping her, burning her, and suffocating her.

She let out a cry, recoiling while sneezing and coughing.

"Oh dear, I thought a ghost had crawled out from under the floor," she said.

Her eyes closed tightly in pain, she groped in the darkness of the fireplace with her blackened hands.

"Ah! I know now," she said with surprise. "The kettle is gone."

"No, I really don't understand why. The kettle was just here. There's no mistake, because I heard it chirping like a flute," she said.

The kettle had been taken away while Orolin had turned her back to empty vegetable peels out the window.

But who took it?

The Raypeak family, looking solemn and calm, appeared on the straw mat at the bedroom doorway.

"Making such a commotion, Orolin!"

"You call this a commotion, you call this a commotion!" Orolin cried. "How could I not make a commotion after such a ghostly thing happened! I almost got burned.

Look at my wooden shoes, my skirt, my hands. My pockets are full of coal dust." (To be continued)

Talks

Three Weeks Six O'Clock

— Niu

Our country originally had the riddle of "The Hour of Yu on the Twenty-first Day." The "Hour of Yu on the Twenty-first Day" refers to the character "醋" (vinegar). The men and women of our country, unlike those in Russia, are not open in their relationships and are inherently very jealous. Men treat women as a forbidden indulgence, and women treat men as a forbidden indulgence. Therefore, if one side engages in extramarital activities, the other side becomes acidic. Now, with a new twist, the expression has changed to "Three Weeks, Six O'Clock," which still means the same as "The Hour of Yu on the Twenty-first Day." I don't understand why people always measure time in three-week increments.

When welcoming important foreign dignitaries with naval gun salutes, twenty-one guns are always fired. During Yuan Shikai's era, the Japanese presented conditions, forcing our country to acknowledge them, also consisting of twenty-one articles. Now, the major sales at major companies and stores in Shanghai also last for twenty-one days in most cases. Even our country's old proverbs say, "Regardless of three times seven is twenty-one." Why not say four times seven is twenty-eight, or four times eight is thirty-two? Why not fire a neat twenty guns in a gun salute? Why not propose twenty, thirty, or forty conditions, instead of an odd twenty-one? The same goes for store sales. Why must they last for twenty-one days? I originally had no idea about the reasoning behind this.

It just so happens that I've discovered another twenty-one-day instance: Mahatma Gandhi, the leader of the Indian National Congress, began a twenty-one-day fast on May 8th as a protest against the disenfranchisement of the untouchable caste. I truly don't understand. Fasting means not eating rice, not eating bread, and avoiding most other foods. However, according to doctors, a strong person who fasts will die in seven days, while a weak person will die in four or five days. How can Gandhi's fast be scheduled for twenty-one days and still not necessarily lead to death? According to Gandhi, "If the British government does not meet his demands after twenty-one days of fasting, he is willing to go to prison." This kind of fasting is very strange. Perhaps the method of fasting is not abrupt but rather, like friends quitting smoking, reduced day by day.

Gandhi's fast reminded me of our comrade, Young Marshal Zhang, who also fasted in Shanghai for twenty-one days and also did not die. This is truly strange. Isn't our comrade Young Marshal Zhang known as the Gandhi of our country? Because Gandhi advocates the "non-resistance" doctrine, and Young Marshal Zhang advocates the "non-resistance" doctrine. Regardless of whether one is a citizen of a fallen country and the other is a young marshal with soldiers and guns who has not yet lost his country, whether they should hold the same doctrine is debatable. But since their doctrines are similar, it is appropriate to consider him the Gandhi of our country.

Not only does Young Marshal Zhang share Gandhi's doctrine, but even in the matter of fasting, he is identical to Gandhi. It is said that Young Marshal Zhang's trip abroad to Italy is partly for rest and partly to promote our country's prestige abroad. According to the Young Marshal himself, he intends to return to serve the country after resting abroad. It is commendable to not forget national salvation even while enjoying leisure. However, because Italy does not have a public monopoly on opium, nor is there private domestic opium available, he decided to fast for twenty-one days in Shanghai due to these inconveniences. During this fasting period, it was said to be very dangerous, but fortunately, it was successfully overcome thanks to the proper medical treatment of a certain doctor. However, according to inquiries, the Young Marshal used as many as twenty-one nurses (or nineteen according to one account) during this fast, and the cost of the fast reached as high as 210,000 yuan (or 200,000 according to one account). This kind of fasting is truly more meaningful than that of Mahatma Gandhi.

Literature and Art

The Legacy in the Stone Casket

— Master of West River

The jade casket and golden seal established the nation's principles,

The legacy of the Western Zhou lasts ten thousand years.

Buddhist monks uniquely praise our party,

A new villa is built as a Buddhist retreat.

A shocking revelation leaves regrets,

May the sound of bells and shadows of monks be boundless.

Alas, North China is still full of troubles,

Who can maintain order when a single hair hangs by a thousand pounds?

The Heat of Youth

— Yi Ping

"Look, this cheongsam is too short, not even covering the heels of my shoes. The color isn't pretty either. It should be bright red, isn't everyone wearing bright red?" She said, casually taking off the cheongsam and throwing it on the bed, then trying on a new one.

She pretended to be very unhappy and glared at the young man who was waiting for her to leave. "This cheongsam is too loose at the waist. It would be so embarrassing to wear it out. I'm not going." She deliberately took off the cheongsam again, and in front of the mirror, wiggled her butt and turned around, striking a dancing pose.

"If it doesn't fit right, it doesn't matter. If you don't like it, we'll make a new one tomorrow. It's getting late. Let's go see 'The Heat of Youth'!" the young man pleaded, his eyes fixed on the flesh beneath her undershirt, fantasizing about the steps he would take in the dark cinema.

"No, no, no..." she said with a sidelong glance and feigned anger, tapping the floor with her high-heeled shoes.

"I promise you, we'll make another bright red one, my dear sister!" He hugged her body like a hungry tiger pouncing on its prey and kissed her wildly.

Struggle, resistance.

"Who cares about your 'coming'?" She said coyly, looking at her apple-red face in the mirror.

"I didn't say you wanted it, we are friends, offering another red dress based on friendship... haha... to strengthen our bond," he said, smiling with satisfaction. His wide mouth stretched out towards her apple cheeks, but she deliberately dodged it. He moved even more boldly closer.

"Annoying..." a muffled voice.

"Let's go, it's getting late." A triumphant return.

He opened the stiff collar of the new cheongsam. Like a marble boy, she still twisted her waist, halfheartedly, before finally slipping her white lotus arms into the sleeves.

The figures in the mirror resumed their work. A youthful couple, hand in hand, stepped out of the door, greeted by a warm early summer breeze.

"Why is it so hot?" Artificial eyebrows furrowed as she spoke.

"Shall we go to the Jardin de la Salle after?"

A nod of agreement.

He was the son of a bank president, with plenty of money at home. His parents had specially built him a body like a bull. This bull was the standard young man of 1933. He had been in a certain university for three years, and his time spent in the classroom was probably measured in hours, but at every sports meet, his records were particularly numerous. His photos appeared in every sports publication and newspaper. The school, in order to ensure he won every sports championship, had almost allowed him to graduate. She was the queen of his school, and many effeminate boys who traded in jade-like items had been manipulated by her and become weary of it. Therefore, with the social skills of a queen, she had seized the bull for herself. Besides a certain satisfaction, there was also a bank behind him. This was the reason the queen was hanging on the young man's arm.

He hadn't expected that the bull's luck would turn in 1933. The innate shortcomings he had previously thought of could now win a woman's heart, and he effortlessly embraced the queen with his wealth.

They walked slowly along the sidewalk, entering the cinema twenty minutes later. The young and mature female lead smiled at the foreign bull, revealing her white legs.

In the darkness, they both felt a satisfying comfort.

Page 20

He thought: "The bull is a great object of female attention!"

She: "To manipulate a man, you only need to flash a white leg!"

The Most Effective National Salvation Policy

— Jie Lu

丨Castration for National Salvation Theory丨

Who doesn't shout "China is weak!" "China is poor!" Why is it so weak and poor? There must be a reason. Therefore, the patriotic people who have invented "dancing for national salvation," "aviation for national salvation," "broadsword for national salvation," "movies for national salvation," etc., etc., have each offered their grand ideas, opening up a scheme to save China from poverty and weakness. Whether they are correct or not, we will have to wait and see the effects in the future. Whether they are effective or not, there is no guarantee of a refund.

According to my humble opinion, the most effective national salvation policies are only two words: one is "heart" and the other is "sex." No matter how good the theory is, if there is hypocrisy, it will be ineffective. Doctrines, speeches, and plans all belong to the "human problem." Without "integrity" and "conscience," good things cannot be done. Therefore, after a boycott, there must be a group of people without "integrity" and "conscience" who will profit from it. Therefore, I say that doctrines and plans cannot save the country and may even accelerate its demise. Second, I say "sex" for national salvation. Does this mean that if our country has a few more sexology professors like Mr. Zhang Jingsheng, the country will be saved? In this era of love and carnality, even the literary masters who bear the great mission of cultural movement are trying their best to promote sexology, so why should I speak further? However, what I am saying about "sex for national salvation" is not fabricated and is indeed based on fact. According to a Berlin telegraph on May 5th:

"The National Socialist government is currently considering a new law that all criminals and those with physical or mental disabilities will be rendered unable to reproduce, and interracial marriage will be prohibited in order to improve the Aryan race." Originally, pigs and boars have the most astonishing birth rate, only knowing "eating" and "reproducing" without doing anything else, and it is not a pity if they are slaughtered. The same is true for the people of our country. "Eating" aside, the ability to "reproduce" is also admirable. Is it because poor friends do not have the fortune to study the sexology of concubines and are just finding poor fun with their yellow-faced wives? They do not know that the poorer they are, the more they reproduce, and the more they reproduce, the poorer they become. Rural bankruptcy, economic panic, and the global depression all stem from this. It is not unique to China!

According to biologists, "The human reproduction rate is a geometric progression, doubling every twenty-five years." Reading history, after decades or centuries, there will inevitably be great chaos, which is iron proof of overpopulation. Moreover, although we Chinese may have weak physiques, we are very vigorous in reproduction, not caring about the spread of flawed offspring. Hitler was able to promulgate new laws in Germany, using methods to prevent criminals and people with physical disabilities from reproducing, which is truly the only way to enrich the country and strengthen the race. Therefore, I have come up with a good strategy for national salvation, which is the "eunuch national salvation argument." I wonder if the officials will adopt my humble suggestion?

A Trip to the Park

— Bei

"This is paradise, glorious paradise!"

Escaping from the piles of life, dragging my heavy body, I approached the entrance of ×× Park. I couldn't help but praise it in this way. Seeing my anxious and almost frantic appearance, the gatekeeper blocked the threshold, repeatedly shouting "Pass! Pass! " a third "Pass!".

"This is paradise, glorious paradise!"

Finding my way inside, my muscles relaxed, and my soul seemed to float in space. I praised it again in this way.

Here, the emotion that floated to my mind was the "croak, croak, croak" of frogs clamoring in the park's pond. So I stopped in my tracks and began a new contemplation: My hometown, five thousand miles away, isn't it precisely at this time when the frogs croak loudly across the fields? Why has it become a bad omen, like the hooting of an owl at midnight or the cawing of a crow in the morning, foreboding ill? Regardless of gender or age, everyone has left their homes and fields, drifting far away to a foreign land, leaving only my father to guard it in his labored breathing. Are the frogs still croaking at this time? And what kind of tone are they croaking in?

Expanding it further: The cries of the thirty million compatriots in the Northeast, the sound of the righteous army's bloody battles against the enemy, must also be croaking like frogs, but who is listening? Who has ever heard them?

"Look, isn't that someone tailing someone else in front? A man following a woman!" Brother Xi reminded me, oh, the park is such a kind of stage. With trailing, with love, it's probably inevitable that there will be a third kind, like the human flesh trade in the Xinxin Bridge area. I even remembered that the wife of the ×× philosopher was tailed from here, and the lovers of ×× classmate also became a family tailed from here.

"Ah, this is even more a paradise of romance!" I changed my first praise.

Not even walking a full circle, in the thick shade of trees on Lafayette Road, came a "giggle, giggle" sound, a pair of angels embracing, kissing wildly, exchanging soul and flesh.

Sitting on the edge of the pond, facing the "splash, splash" of ducks hitting the water, that sound mixed with sweet whispers and songs, undulating on the water of the pond. It was a time for the park visitors to be intoxicated.

Where there is good in the world, there must be evil. Where there are lovely beautiful scenes, there are bound to be unexpected disappointments that spoil the scenery. One small stone after another was thrown in from outside the fence, obviously from those who were rejected outside feeling unfair, and the number of visitors gradually dwindled.

Although the weather was very good, there was no sign of the crescent moon. The moon, the bright moon, was only peeking through the dense clouds. Near Hualong Road, a new bathhouse was under construction. Under the white-hot electric lights, the workers were "bang, bang, bang" releasing the clanging sound of hammers and stones. When we slipped out from the relatively relaxed gaze of the gatekeeper, a storm was already urgently approaching.

Picking Up Gold

— Yan Ye

Splendid mansions, beautiful clothes, delicious delicacies, beautiful wives and concubines - these are all children of gold. Whoever obtains gold can enjoy these four, and more, superior forms of life. If you want to enjoy this kind of life, please come to Shanghai. Gold is everywhere in Shanghai, just waiting to be picked up. Are readers skeptical? Listen to me!

Golden Barrel Grand Champagne, first prize 420,000, second prize 120,000, third prize 60,000, small prizes totaling 150,000. The fundraising amount for the Yu, Anhui, and Hubei disaster relief efforts totals 1,000,000 yuan, with prize money accounting for three-quarters of it. With so many opportunities to win prizes, isn't this gold for anyone to pick up? Aviation Highway Lottery, first prize 500,000 yuan, and the smaller prizes below are also more than the Golden Barrel lottery. The fundraising amount totals 5,000,000 yuan, scattering 3,000,000 yuan in prizes all over Shanghai, making the opportunity to pick it up even greater. In the past, someone picked up 200 yuan in the seven characters of "One Branch Seven Clever Ten Li Fragrance". Someone also picked up huge sums of money from the Pylon Guessing Game. Now, awaiting people to pick up, the Lux Soap Cigarette is electing a movie queen with a top prize of 2,000 yuan, the White Gold Dragon Cigarette, if you get all the poem riddles right, it has 500 yuan, the Company Brand Cigarette, twenty empty boxes in exchange for a top prize of 2,000 yuan, the Swirling Palace Brand Cigarette, twenty empty boxes in exchange for 500 yuan, and a certain bookstore is giving away racetrack tickets with book purchases. In addition, there are various ways of scattering gold. It's impossible to remember and write about everything at once. It's like this now, and there will be even more in the future, which is to be expected. It's also conceivable that layers of gold will pile up on the ground in Shanghai.

The above-mentioned 420,000 and 500,000 top prizes only require an investment of ten yuan to pick up. Other prizes require no capital at all. You can unexpectedly obtain them from items you must purchase in your daily life. In short, it rains gold and gold is everywhere in Shanghai. As long as you have the ability and good luck, you can pick up countless gold coins for you to hunt for splendid mansions, beautiful clothes, delicious delicacies, and beautiful wives and concubines. At the very least, it can save you from a temporary emergency.

My Education

— Lu

(1)

I didn't get what I wanted, so I cried.

"Good baby, don't cry, Grandma will buy you candy later," Grandma said, touching my head. I still didn't stop, I knew she was just哄 (hǒng:哄 is an important verb here meaning to coax or deceive with pleasant words) me.

"Good baby, don't let Dad hear you, or he'll hit you again."

I still kept crying.

"Third Brother, quickly close the door, the foreigners are coming! Third Brother, quickly close the door!" Grandma suddenly shouted. Third Brother really closed the door. "Baby isn't here, Baby isn't crying, foreigners don't come here. My Baby is really good, he's not crying!"

I was scared and buried my head in Grandma's arms, quickly stopping my crying.

(2)

"Mom, the neighbor's son, A'Niu, hit me and stole my toy gun!" I cried, telling Mom.

"Good-for-nothing! Who told you to hang out with that little rogue? Who's going to pity you?" Mom scolded fiercely, pulling me out of the hall and taking the rattan whip, pretending to hit me.

"You little rogue, a nobody's kid who doesn't get disciplined, you hit people? You steal people's toy guns? Good, I won't let you off today, you little rogue!"

Mom pretended to hit me again, but I wasn't afraid. I knew Mom was using me to scold A'Niu.

A'Niu's mother heard this and also rushed out, scolding A'Niu.

"Did you steal someone else's stuff again? Quickly take it out. Where's the toy gun I bought for you a few days ago? Worthless thing! You lose your own things and then steal someone else's!"

Mom and A'Niu's mother argued for a long time before they stopped.

(3)

The time was autumn. The trees outside the courtyard were scattered by the wind, and many children were picking up fallen leaves to play with. I was very happy to see them and quietly opened the door to go out, but Mom saw me, grabbed my hand, and scolded:

"It's windy outside, you'll get sick again!"

"Mom, I want to play with fallen leaves."

"No, it's too dirty."

I cried again, and Mom put a piece of candy in my mouth.

(4)

The gongs and drums were loud outside. Today, "Ox-Head God" was parading through the streets. Mom, my sister, and I watched at the doorway.

"Mom, who is that person with the black face?" I asked, pointing to Mom.

"Don't point, quickly put your palms together and pray."

I put my palms together and prayed. Mom chanted: "The child is ignorant, please Ox-Head God teach him."

Novels

The Life of Wu Ji (8) (Continued)

— Ling He

8. "Just Marry Him"

"Where did you go? I've been waiting for you for ages."

As she stepped into the room, she saw Master Zhang lying on the bed, smoking opium. As soon as he saw her, he happily sat up and said to her with delight.

"Oh!" So she immediately forced a cheerful expression. "Oh, it's you! Where have you been all this time?"

As she sat near the bed, he embraced her. She then pressed his head to her chest, stroked his cheek with one hand, and took the opportunity to wipe away the tears from the corners of her eyes. She said softly:

"I almost died of missing you."

Just this simple sentence pierced Master Zhang's heart, because he hugged her even tighter. Afterward, she was pinned down on the bed, and Master Zhang pressed his whole body onto her, tearing off her clothes buttons as if fighting. After a round of caresses, she finally lay beside him while he smoked opium, exhausted and unable to lift her hands. When she carefully prepared a smoke bubble and was about to put the pipe to his lips, she saw that he was sound asleep. At this moment, she gave him a fierce smile, relieved to put down the pipe and rest.

Suddenly, a burst of angry and pleading voices came from the next room. She could tell that her companions were again suffering assault.

"No, don't do this! ... No ... I'll shout ... Haha ... Ouch ... Haha ... Someone come! ... No ... Someone's coming ... How embarrassing ... Ouch ... Hahahaha ..."

Then there was the sound of smashing bowls and plates, as the woman struggled to resist. Finally, the woman broke free, panting, and ran out the door amid a burst of laughter. Afterward, there was the strangely annoying sound of a huqin.

Miss Liu couldn't help but sigh heavily at this moment. She sat up and ran her hand through her greasy hair, finding that some strands were already out of place. Since she couldn't sleep anyway, she decided to go to the mirror and comb her hair.

She drank a cup of tea and then lit another cigarette, blowing out smoke rings of different sizes. The smaller rings went through the larger ones, and soon they all disappeared.
