Film Special

Did Lili Damita Really Get Married?

— Fu Tou

The only question that fans in Hollywood and across the United States want to know today is whether the beautiful European star Lili Damita is married or not. According to Lili herself, she has not been married or engaged. However, according to rumors from the German Ufa company, Lili Damita is indeed a married woman. Her husband is Willb Fritscb, the male lead who worked with her at Ufa, and they call their marriage "The Fairbanks Pickford Comdination of Europe." The two sides each hold their own, who should people believe?

What evidence does Ufa have for their rumor? It's quite interesting. It is said that two burglars, hearing that Ms. Damita had many diamonds, including one weighing twenty-five carats, decided to pay a visit to Damita's residence in the middle of the night. They climbed up to her apartment from the water pipe and sneaked into her bedroom. Suddenly the lights turned on, and they saw Lili sleeping in bed, in a sweet dream. A man was sitting by the bed, holding a pistol. The two burglars, feeling trapped, remembered that the newspaper had reported that Lili was unmarried, so they said to the man: "Will you let us go or not? If you don't let us go, we will reveal your secret."

"Go ahead, go ahead," the man said with a smile. "I'm not afraid of what the newspapers publish. Miss Damita and I have been secretly married for three months. I am Willb Fritscb, as you probably know." But Willb Fritscb eventually released the two burglars. Later, they told this story to others, and this is the basis for Ufa's claim that Lili is already married.

As soon as Lili Damita arrived in the United States, the first question that American reporters asked her was, "When is your husband coming to meet you?" Lili shook her head and said that she did not have a husband. People then asked her, if she didn't have a husband, why did Ufa say that she did? She said that it was Ufa's publicity stunt, and that the story of the burglars was also for publicity. People also asked her about her friendship with Willb Fritscb. She said, "Willb and I have collaborated in countless films. We work together day and night, performing romance in front of countless fans. Of course, we cannot remain indifferent, but we can perform romance and also break free from romance. When I was young, I even fell in love with a postal worker!"

"I don't know how many times the newspapers have published news of my marriage, I can't even remember. Among those men were dukes, counts, American millionaires, all sorts of people. But I am still free, even more free than the crows flying over my head!"

Lili Damita herself says that she has "no preconceived notions" about marriage on this trip to the United States. She admires American men. She says that American men are better than those in Berlin, not only are they better looking, but they are also smarter and more lively, unlike men from other countries. She feels comfortable and at ease among American men, without any restraint. She says that American women are also better looking than European women, with slender figures and beautiful faces.

Audience Opinions

Discussion of "Blood Letter"

— Yu Hong

After "The Great Man" and "Her Heart", the Moon Light Company's "Blood Letter" has already been released at the Central Theater. I still take in this new work with the passion of cherishing domestic films. Although it still doesn't completely satisfy me, it is at least better than before. However, the consciousness in the story is still an ordinary love pursuit, and it cannot give us any new inspiration. There has also been no progress in terms of technique and expression. Here are some points in the play that I find inappropriate for discussion.

(1) Zhong Yuqing gives Yu Juan a small photo with the words "Yu Juan, my love" written on it. And her brother, Niu Er, insists on taking it for himself, even though he is said to be simple and foolish, it is still too artificial.

(2) After escaping from the fire pit, Yu Juan risks her life to find Yuqing, and suddenly encounters an "elephant" on the way. It is rare to have such wild animals in such a close place to the city, and the "elephant" has a huge ring in its nose, obviously kept by someone. In my opinion, this section is completely unnecessary.

(3) Yu Juan chews her finger to write a blood letter in the inn and swallows gold to commit suicide, but she is still alive at the grand reunion. How she was rescued is not explained, which is the biggest loophole.

(4) Yuqing takes Niu Er to Mo Zuomin's villa at night, jumps onto the roof, and walks like the wind, which has the flavor of old novels, and is a poisonous legacy of outdated films with great destruction and arson, which is disheartening.

(5) The furnishings in the room, such as the telephone and sofa, are extremely luxurious, while the outdoor scene is desolate with weeds and wild trees, making people wonder if it is a city or a remote village? The costumes are also very contradictory.

(6) The synopsis says that Yu Juan spent the night in an ancient temple, frightened by a thief, and obtained silver as travel expenses. But there is no such scene in the film. When Zuomin was killed, the synopsis said that the family members came out one after another, but there is no such fact in the film. All these are due to the director's lack of careful planning. If the audience does not read the synopsis, they will not know what it is about.

The above points are not impossible to remedy, and I hope the director will also correct them.

The Star Company's sound film "Powder Market" will soon be released at the New Light Theater. The director of the film is Mr. Zhang Shichuan, starring Hu Die, Gong Jianong, Yan Yuexian, etc.

Alice's Adventures in Wonderland

To be Made into a Movie

The famous novel "Alice's Adventures in Wonderland" by Lewis Carroll will be made into a movie in Hollywood, with Mary Pickford playing the role of Alice. Douglas Fairbanks was in Rome riding a car to participate in the Italian Golf Champagne Competition. A Reuters reporter made a special visit to him. According to Fairbanks, the film is full of peaceful and serene air, and will be a new look in film dramas. In the play, only Pickford is the only real person, and the rest are dummies. Fairbanks said that he hopes to come to China to shoot the film next time, but all the equipment must be moved from Hollywood to the East, so at least one hundred and ten thousand yuan will be needed. However, judging from the current film market, it may be difficult to bear such a huge amount, etc. (Reuters Rome)

Recent Domestic Films to be Released

— Yi Yi

The General Trend of Film Themes

Since this time the film industry has had a revival opportunity, the domestic film industry has suddenly shown a booming atmosphere; and the general audience has also shifted their attention from Hollywood films, and expressed a grand and enthusiastic welcome to domestic films. Recently, according to my investigation, there will be four domestic films released in this district, which I will introduce to the readers below:

(1) Star Company's "Powder Market", directed by Zhang Shichuan, starring Hu Die, Gong Jianong, Yan Yuexian, etc. It will be released at the New Light Theater on the 14th of this month.

(2) Star Company's "Future", directed by Zhang Shichuan, starring Xuan Jinglin, Sun Min, Zhu Qiuhen, etc., will be released simultaneously at the Central Theater in Shanghai within the next ten days, the exact date is undetermined.

(3) Lianhua Company's "New Year's Eve", directed by Jiang Qifeng, starring Chen Yanyan, Liu Jiqun, Jiang Junchao; there is news that it will be released on the same day as "Powder Market" in Beijing.

(4) Tianyi Company's "Vitality", directed by Shao Zuiweng, starring Chen Yumei, Yuan Meiyun, Zhang Zhenduo; it will be released within ten days, the exact date is undetermined.

Of the above four films, two are sound films and two are silent films. One thing to note is that, except for the plot of "New Year's Eve" which the reporter is not very clear about, the other three films are all about women's issues. From this, we can see that since the release of "The Cry of Women", the theme of domestic films, "women's issues", seems to have become a general trend.

"Where to Go?"

— Yin

Art China Film Company's Debut Work

Art China Film Company's debut work, "Where to Go?" formerly titled "Homeless Chinese People", the whole play takes the suffering of the general people during the period from "September 18th" to "January 28th" as the theme, writing out the cruelty and conspiracy of international imperialists in oppressing weak nations. The screenwriter and director are both Mr. Chen Yu. In addition to wrestlers such as Zha Ruilong and Peng Fei, well-known ladies from the drama world such as Jinxiu Wen, Hong Dou, and Lei Mengna have also joined in cooperation. It is now heard that the film has completed the last scene - the war scene - yesterday.

Letter to the Editor

To the editor, in the "Shanghai News in Brief" published in your esteemed publication on the ninth of this month, it was mentioned that Xue Juexian was very disappointed after Bai Jinlong was banned. After investigation, the Bai Jinlong film was co-produced by our company and Mr. Xue. Since it was submitted to the Film Inspection Committee for inspection, it has never been banned. We hereby correct this and kindly request that the original letter be published as is.

A Collection of Local Intelligence

— Zhou Jingzhi

Lianhua's "Maternal Light" has been filming for more than a month, and yesterday they went to Hangzhou to take external scenes. This external scene is the scenery of the Nanyang mining area, so they brought a lot of Nanyang trees to plant, in order to be realistic.

Jinan Company's sound film "Winning Glory for the Country" has been completed. This film is a combination of martial arts and love. It will be able to meet the people of Shanghai soon.

A pair of comedic old partners - Hoersay and Wheeler - arrived in Shanghai the day before yesterday and ran to Yiwei to dance. Coincidentally, our Queen Hu Die was also dancing gracefully, so this pair of comedic old partners looked at her carefully as if they had discovered a new continent, but Hu Die was a little shy.

The foreign films that will be coming to Shanghai soon include "So Africa", co-starring Hoersay and Wheeler, "Sailor's Luck", co-starring James Dunn and Sally Eilers, and "42nd Street", starring Bebe Daniels and Warner Baxter.

Star Company's "Iron Plate Red Tears Record" is nearing completion. It is heard that the new film after this film is "On the Fuchun River", directed by Hong Shen.

Lianhua Company has recently produced a "Shanghai Grand View", the content of which is entirely Shanghai scenes. The results are quite impressive. It is heard that it will be released with the main film soon.

The Secrets (7) of the Film Novel

— Cairo

"Mary!" John shouted outside. "Shenxiang is hurt, come quickly!"

Mary seemed to wake up from a dream. She quickly put Little John's stiff body into the cradle; straightened up, wiped the tears from her eyes with the back of her hand, and ran out. She was bandaging Shenxiang's wound when suddenly the house was filled with thick smoke. She looked up at the skylight on the roof and saw Red-Faced Jack climbing on the skylight, one hand holding a torch setting fire, and the other hand holding a pistol ready to open fire on John. As if divinely inspired, Mary quickly took Shenxiang's gun from the side and fired at Red-Faced Jack with a bang. Red-Faced Jack fell in from the skylight like a dead crow and died on the ground.

Outside the door, there was the sound of horses galloping. Then there were shouts and gunshots. After listening for a while, John suddenly shouted happily, "That's Dr. McGoffin, bringing the local police!" This new force beat the gang of cattle thieves to pieces, and they fled in all directions. A fierce battle that was almost on the verge of danger also came to an end. John also won a complete victory. Mary's contribution, of course, was also considerable.

The next day, John and Mary buried Little John's body in joy and sorrow, came back to repair the house, tidy up the utensils, and prepared to recreate the family.

It seemed that heaven was afraid that their love was not strong, so it deliberately added various hardships; after they had gone through many trials and dangers, their love could not be shaken at all, so "heaven's heart" also turned around. Since the fierce battle with Red-Faced Jack, John's luck has turned. From then on, everything went smoothly, and John's wealth and reputation increased a thousand miles a day. After Little John died, Little William was born, and Otterley, Susan, and Robert were born one after another. At this time, Shenxiang, the children called him Old Uncle, was no longer an employee, but a member of the John Caton family, receiving extremely preferential treatment. But Shenxiang had one thing.

He hated the fact that whenever there was a banquet, he had to wear a formal suit with a stiff collar, which made his movements and breathing very uncomfortable. He thought to himself that for the sake of Mary and John, he was not afraid to go through fire and water; what he was most afraid of was formal attire with a stiff collar.

This day was another day of a grand banquet. Caton had been nominated as the candidate for governor of California, and this was the first celebration dance. Shenxiang also wore a formal suit and walked around among the guests, listening to the announcer announcing the names of the distinguished guests. Suddenly, a beautiful Spanish young woman came in, and the announcer announced her name, "Miss Martinez." Shenxiang happened to be standing next to a pair of male and female guests. He heard them whispering. The woman said, "How dare she be so bold!" The man said, "Caton is crazy, bringing this kind of woman into his house!"

Shenxiang looked around for John and Mary. John looked ashamed, Mary also felt uneasy, and Miss Martinez was approaching the hosts. (To be continued)
